Pali: Moghapucchakena cāti. [47]

Pali: saraṇehi dhammehi ye dhammā vippayuttā … 

dt2.14:62.6
Pali: te dhammā asaṅkhataṁ khandhato ṭhapetvā pañcahi khandhehi dvādasahāyatanehi aṭṭhārasahi dhātūhi saṅgahitā. 

dt2.14:62.7
Pali: Katihi asaṅgahitā? 

dt2.14:62.8
Pali: Na kehici khandhehi na kehici āyatanehi na kāhici dhātūhi asaṅgahitā. 

dt2.14:63.1
Pali: Na rūpāvacarehi dhammehi ye dhammā … 

dt2.14:63.2
Pali: na arūpāvacarehi dhammehi ye dhammā … 

dt2.14:63.3
Pali: aniyyānikehi dhammehi ye dhammā … 

dt2.14:63.4
Pali: aniyatehi dhammehi ye dhammā … 

dt2.14:63.5
Pali: araṇehi dhammehi ye dhammā vippayuttā, te dhammā katihi khandhehi katihāyatanehi katihi dhātūhi saṅgahitā? 

dt2.14:63.6
Pali: Te dhammā catūhi khandhehi dvīhāyatanehi dvīhi dhātūhi saṅgahitā. 

dt2.14:63.7
Pali: Katihi asaṅgahitā? 

dt2.14:63.8
Pali: Ekena khandhena dasahāyatanehi soḷasahi dhātūhi asaṅgahitā. 

dt2.14:64.1
Pali: Dhammāyatanaṁ dhammadhātu, 

dt2.14:64.2
Pali: Atha jīvitaṁ nāmarūpaṁ; 

dt2.14:64.3
Pali: Saḷāyatanaṁ jātijarāmataṁ, 

dt2.14:64.4
Pali: Dve ca tike na labbhare. 

dt2.14:65.1
Pali: Paṭhamantare satta ca, 

dt2.14:65.2
Pali: Gocchake dasa aparante; 

dt2.14:65.3
Pali: Cuddasa cha ca matthake, 

dt2.14:65.4
Pali: Iccete sattacattālīsa dhammā; 

dt2.14:65.5
Pali: Samucchede na labbhanti, 

dt2.14:65.6
Pali: Moghapucchakena cāti. [47] 

dt2.14:66.1
Pali: Vippayuttenasaṅgahitāsaṅgahitapadaniddeso cuddasamo. 

dt2.14:67.1
Pali: Dhātukathāpakaraṇaṁ niṭṭhitaṁ.
